<Text>Delicious. Fresh. Great service. Reasonable price. Got the set meal for $35 (which the waitress did note the cuts are better than if you got the combos). Also ordered their homemade tofu which was super soft and yummy, the Spanish mackerel which not only served picture-worthy but also very delicious (pricey but worth it). Also ordered a sashimi over rice which I felt compared to the other cuts, were not as great. They also serve green tea and mochi at the end. Really awesome experience and delicious sushi. Totally satisfied my craving. < Text>
First time customers, and we will definitely come back! My mom can only eat gluten free food, and the waitresses & owner or manager made sure that the things she ate were gluten-free. They were so sweet and accommodating.
The sashimi combo plate was fresh, the grilled salmon was delicious! The seaweed salad was more like interesting seaweeds/iceberg combo salad. The meat was tender.
The dessert we chose was the pudding, like flan! Super yummy, made in-house.
Prices are reasonable.
Free parking next door under the Landmark theaters.
One suggestion: The shellac on the tables is a little bit sticky feeling.<//Text>

My wife and i first came to this location while it was called Torafuku in 2009 while getting a passport renewed.  We absolutely loved the food, decore, reasomable price, portions and the staff were super.
Fast forward 10 years and alot can change, we came out from our home in AZ to renew a passport again and thought we would spend the day as we did 10 years ago..

The place is now called Wadastumi and i really wished i never crossed the threshold.  We decided to give the new ownership a chance and even after being seated and noticing the sticky tables, upholstery coming apart and dirty blinds along with carpet that was beyond shampooing ....no worries i have had great experiences in worse conditions !  But the food was barely palatable rice for sushi was warm fish was room temp.  The only thing i have that was postitive was wait staff were super nice and polite.  Sorry folks i would say spend your dollars else where.< /Text>

<text>Oh El Pollo Pio Pio. Everything on the menu is wonderful. The food is prepared by hand by who I assume are the mother and father of the most friendly and polite children that often man the counter. I love this place, not only is the food delicious - but the care taken with preparation of the food and the cleanliness of the restaruant and the way the family interacts with each other makes the whole experience special. It's like coming to visit your mother or grandmother and they've made your favorite food. It is really that good.

But, my favorite part of coming here is the soup. My mother passed away some time ago. I miss her dearly. Her and I would always go find awessome soup places or make homemade soup together. That was "our" thing to do. She'd love the soup here. Chicken, beef, pozole or menudo - it's so very delicious. And all the soups come with fresh garnishes of onion, cilantro, lemon and jalapenos. As if that was not enough - every soup comes with the best hand made corn tortillas you've every had.

The love this mother has for her children. The love this family has for each other and the hard work they put into this business comes through in the soup (though it's present in the chicken too). It always helps fill the hole I have in my heart, just a little bit, and remember the good times I had with my mother each time I order a bowl. I'm so very thankful for this place and the food they so lovingly serve.< /text><user_id>106556599472578764154</user_id><pictures>None</pictures><Name>Hayden Bond< /Name>< gmap_id>

<text>AUTOPOM REALLY DELIVERS ON THEIR WARRANTIES

Although we have been very lucky in terms of service on our most recent Range Rovers, we decided to purchase extended warranties just in case we had an issue prior to trading them in for the new model.  The search for the most comprehensive and reliable extended warranty though, was not the easiest of tasks given that there were many options in the market.  Numerous companies, including some of the largest names on television, promise the most comprehensive policies and hassle free service, but after reading hundreds of reviews, it was clear that many of the companies do not stand behind their guarantees.  After a long and exhaustive search and although their reviews were actually great to begin with, we took a leap of faith and selected AutoPom.

AutoPom has several different plans, but because Range Rovers are notorious for costly repairs when something does go wrong, we selected the EFG platinum plan, which I was told is as close to the original factory warranty as possible.  After a little more than 2 years into extended warranty and despite the fact that my wife‚Äôs car is barely ever driven and still only has 26,000 miles on it, we heard a strange noise coming from the engine and therefore decided to send the car in to be checked out.  The Range Rover repair facility provided a long list of required repairs totaling just over $18,000 and mentioned that they would contacting AutoPom directly to start the claims process.

Because of the huge costs involved, AutoPom sent out an inspector to survey the vehicle and it was the inspector‚Äôs expert opinion that the vast majority of the items on the list were unnecessary since most were in perfect working order.  I contacted the service department and AutoPom to discuss the discrepancy and quickly realized what might have been going on. Suffice to say, I was furious that the repair shop seemed to be attempting to take advantage of me and the warranty company by running up the cash register with numerous items that appeared to be unnecessary. That issue has already been resolved appropriately.

In the end though, there were three or four items that were actually necessary, the total cost of which was approximately $5000.  AutoPom covered everything exactly as they promised they would before I purchased their warranty and stood behind their promises without delay or denial.  Additionally, the fact that they sent their own inspector out to survey the vehicle before the repairs started served as an important check because had I not had an advocate with them, I could have unfortunately been the victim of a large bill that was almost entirely unnecessary.  I wanted to also mention that when the claim started, I had no issues reaching their team and I was even able to speak with the owner of the company who very generously, offered to step in and assist me with the situation.

If  my memory serves me correctly, I believe the total cost of the warranty was about $3500 for three additional years and it has obviously already paid for itself 1 ¬Ω times over.  I could not be happier with the AutoPom guarantee and their very professional, knowledgeable and courteous team who were in my corner looking out for my interests as well, from the moment they were contacted.

If you are in need of an extended warranty, you should consider my review of AutoPom as a truly real life and honest firsthand experience of their wonderful company!</text><pics>None<//pics><Response>{'time': 1612245502243, 'text': 'Thank you Jeffrey for taking the time to share your story. \xa0Very much appreciated! \xa0It was a pleasure assisting you with your claim. \xa0Your review illustrates what we call "The autopom! < Text>
Outback still thinks it's cool to "stick-it" to their customers. There were 3 in our party. Mama had French Onion Soup with a blue cheese salad. I had Prime Rib, 13 Oz with Blue cheese salad and baked potato and Dad had Porter-house with Blue cheese salad and baked potato. We all had drinks. I had a Long Island ice tea, mama had a Tanqueray gin and tonic and dad had a Tanqueray gin and tonic. Take a look at the pictures below. The empry glass was the first long island that they comped because I had to send it back. They forgot to put booze in the first one. There is an example of a full one in the other picture.That is a US Quarter in my fingers. The gin and tonics were 9 dollars and that long island was 8 dollars. You can also see what size the water glass is. Not sure what kind of game they are playing, but I would be embarrassed. Drink size matters. I didn't ask for samples of the drinks!  This is Elk Grove, not Las Vegas! It'll be a little while before we go back to the Outback Steakhouse! $104 dollars for the entire experience is pretty steep! Thank God our waitress understood our pain. My Dad left his business card with the hostess and requested a call from the manager. We'll see how that goes....</Text>

<Review>You just gotta love a primo cut of beef that melts in your mouth. The "Prime Ministers Prime Rib" is at its best when rare, medium rare, or medium. It comes with an jou & choice of creamy horse-radish or chunky (more traditional) horse- radish. They are all very good but the chunky had one hell of a bite! A spicy bite.
The wait staff was impeccable as always. Kind, friendly, patient, knowledgeable, accommodating, and the definition of professionalism.
Great food. Great people. Great experience. Every single time I go there. It's no wonder it's in my "top 5" favorite steakhouse style restaurants in the 916 area.
Give it a try, it's worth it. And besides, who knows, maybe it'll be in your "top 5" faves as well!
Thanks for dinner Outback! It was DELICIOUS!!  (date:03/20/2019)

<review>My first time at outback was a success. I'd been hesitant to go for years, as it seemed like any other diner chain (Applebees, Sharis, etc.), and I'd have to say that I was satiated, but not impressed nor thrilled; very indecisive about how I felt. (+1) for the Appearance. It was decently clean and smelled nice and fresh. Honestly, I'd like to take a point for the lack of server interaction, but there was some redeeming qualities that negated the point I was thinking about revoking, so (+/- 0). I know it's not 'this' specific location's fault, but I'm still not with the tablet devices you can order and pay with. With those working busser/waiter/server positions, their attention is much more spread out because individual tables require less attention, however I'll negate the point I revoked  because the waiter was absolutely gorgeous. I'm just upset I didn't get the opportunity to ask for his # :/
(+1) for the food. My steak with sauteed mushrooms was very average, but the Blooming onion deserves the point alone. (+1) for the audio level in the restaurant. It was nice and quiet, there was no unruly/loud customers, and everybody did their best to uphold the relaxing ambiance. Great work from the customers and staff alike for regulating that. I'd like to end it off with a (+1) because they didn't charge me extra for coffee refills and to prepare extra marinade for my steak after they already brought it out. Wise move on the management, you guys have earned my respect :)
Would absolutely return if my Grandparents were to come into town, as it provides an intimate experience with those you come in with without too much waiter interaction or distracting factors (Such as blinding lighting and loud, boisterous people), but It's not somewhere I'd return to with a group of friends on a night out.<//review><pics>None<//pics><Resp>None< /Resp><gmap_id>0x809ac649069dd60d:0xb14526be4b0d91c8<//gmap_id></record>

For the price of the dish and the cut of the meat I would expect absolutely no grizzle or fat but I was disappointed to find some.
